Loyalty Tests in the Bureaucracy
The Nationalist Government's bureaucracy is bloated and nepotistic, built for patronage and rewarding loyalists rather than administrative efficiency. Now, with allegiances being called in question across the regime, it is time that we begin restacking the government in our favour. The new civil service ought to be qualified, diligent and obey our directives without question!
Promise a Constitutional Government
In a nation that has long been seen as backwards, violent, and effectively feudal, there has been a cry from inside and out for modernisation. The Political Science Clique is eager to demonstrate its commitment to modernity - modern industry, modern styles, modern business culture, modern technology, modern management. Chipping away at needless traditions and turning a new page is a difficult process, but a necessary one.\n\nAmid the chaos of the Hu Hanmin Crisis, there is a growing consensus that the arbitrary, capricious nature of military rule must end in favour of a civilian led government. In place of military dominance, a modern technocratic and responsible government must rise even if it might be too soon for a full democracy. Rule of law, not a party-state and its fanatics, must be the basis of our republic.
Release Political Prisoners
As Hu Hanmin was arrested, hundreds of his followers were detained with him and held without trial. Others were swept up over the years, sometimes on spurious or non-existent charges by an overzealous secret police or turned in by vindictive political rivals. A surefire way of winning over the bourgeoisie and intelligentsia that make up much of the recently elected National Assembly is to release political dissidents who are like them or even close to them. It will not be easy by any means, but it would be a nice starting point for further negotiations.
Bribe Military Officers
The National Revolutionary Army is a heavily politicised force by design, meant to be thoroughly loyal to the party-state and its revolutionary creed. Many of its core divisions and officers are ideological fanatics and thoroughly embedded into the Whampoa cult of personality. However, as the army expanded, they quickly became surrounded by many units freshly absorbed from defeated or integrated warlord armies or new recruits from less politicised training programs. While it might be too late to defang the army altogether, with some carefully placed bribes (both monetary and with regards to promotions) and leveraging our connections to prominent regional military men might be sufficient in deterring less zealous officers from endorsing a coup d'etat.
Call a Vote of No Confidence
The Political Science government has run its course, and not one day too soon. As the treacherous Zhang Qun and two-faced Yang Yongtai flail about, the revolutionary government we have worked so hard to build hurtles towards collapse. Seeing the inevitable and wary of the obvious military discontent, a solid majority over Delegates have been assembled to table discussions on the Provisional Constitution Yang and his allies have staked their legitimacy on. We will press on with a vote of no confidence shortly after and end this farce once and for all.
Increase Propaganda Output
Whampoa has their troops and the Political Science Clique their economic organs, but only the CC Clique can truly harness the will of the people! Through an extensive mass media campaign, with input from the nation's leading thinkers and scholars, we can inflame the hearts and educate minds of the people! With great gusto, we reignite the revolutionary passions of the party!
Stoke Xenophobic Hysteria
Our party is surrounded by party traitors and foreign agents! Syndicalists and their fellow travellers infiltrate and twist our revolution from the left, while the Bank of China's plutocrats and compradors try to buy their way into power from the right! These miscreants have undermined the will of the Chinese people and the spirit of our Nationalist Party, all with the hopes of bringing it under foreign control!\n\nZhang Qun and Yang Yongtai have invited socialists, liberals, reactionaries, and foreign interests into our government under the guise of pluralism, causing nothing but division and ruin! They will soon put our revolution up for auction, and sell our principles to the highest bidder! We will not let them win - all patriots must rise up and meet our obligation to prevent socialist boots from trodding over [ROOT.Capital.GetCapitalVictoryPointName]!
Orchestrate a Walkout of the Bureaucracy
Yang Yongtai, the new Premier, may fancy himself as the new master of the bureaucracy, but the truth is that he has no more power than he has principles. He and his cronies have tried to sift through the administration Dai Jitao has created, slowly shuffling out our appointees and bribing or promoting his own men - creating fear and confusion among the ranks. We will not wait for such indignation - the Chen brothers will orchestrate a mass walkout of government officials, rendering the apparatus inoperable. Even those on the fence will feel the pressure to join our ranks as the Political Science Clique's position grows untenable and our return (and revenge) inevitable.
Mobilise the Political Commissars
Chiang Kai-shek might have built the National Revolutionary Army, but Dai Jitao and Chen Guofu were by his side from the beginning. What makes the National Revolutionary Army different from every other army roaming around China is the thorough political indoctrination imbued into every unit through its political commissars, directly selected and trained by the party itself. It is these connections that we will use to continue to bind the army to us and the good of the party-state.
The Whampoa Coup
A great travesty has occurred - our esteemed Generalissimo was forced to resign by an ungrateful party, thrown out by the likes of the wicked Hu Hanmin. This brazen show of disunity and treachery has made our country look weak on an international stage in a time when the survival of nations depends on vicious strength and tenacity of will. Like the crooked politicians of old, our party has fallen into petty infighting and rivalries over the niceties of a useless piece of paper. If the party cannot sort matters out in a reasonable amount of time, then the revolutionary army that built this nation will take matters into our own hands!
Leverage Whampoa Connections
No matter what has happened, and no matter what will happen, He Yingqin retains a cult of personality. To many former students and staff, he will always be one of the leading instructors of Whampoa, and a venerable revolutionary General that may as well be an institution in of himself. Though only middle aged, he has made his mark on the nation's history. And though boxed in from all sides, there are still many willing to rally behind him.\n\n§RCoaxing the moderates back into his camp will require a more gentlemanly, reassuring approach however, which may set back the army's plans for a coup.§!
Campaign of Intimidation
The nation is at war, whether they realise it or not. Every day is another battle for the security of the nation, and the future of the Chinese race! In this war, every tool in our toolkit must be used to save our country - whether it be assassinations, midnight arrests, and mass surveillance. Through this righteous violence, our nation is reborn.\n\n§RWe must be cautious however, because fear has a tendency to drive frightened men into whichever camp will protect them.§!

Encourage Military Disobedience
Why is our revolution failing today? It surely is not because the army lacks the will to fight. Nor is it because the people lack the fire in their hearts or that China is unable to be a great nation! It is the same reason China has failed the past few centuries - the decadence of the elite and their collusion with foreign powers! While the Beijing sell-outs and Shanghai thieves continue to dominate our politics and economy, there can be no new China. But we will not stand for this, nor will we go back to the way things were!\n\nIt is a dark day when the eternally loyal National Revolutionary Army is called towards disobedience towards the party. But when the entire party apparatus has betrayed the revolution, what else is there to be done? The snakes in the Central Executive Committee have forgotten how indispensable a strong army and a strong hand is in carrying out our revolutionary promises. It is only by organising a mass refusal to follow their illegal orders, destabilising their government, that we can truly save our party and our country!
Negotiate with the SCPC
Hu Hanmin's loyalists have coalesced into a South China Political Council. While we have successfully stemmed their efforts to enlist further support for their movement, they continue to dominate the old party heartland. Either we make a move to reconcile with them (bound to be popular among National Assembly delegates) or we work to undermine these talks.
Handle the Party Left
The Party's left encompasses a broad range of socialists, syndicalists, left nationalists, and progressives and struggle to be a unified entity. Negotiating with them is a difficult task to say the least, it is often akin to talking to a wall. Still, with party unity under question and a growing leftist movement within the army itself, perhaps some arrangement can be made.

The Fight for Human Rights
Forever a perennial struggle is that of the fight for human rights. Not just the citizen's rights, the ones granted to them by by the state, but that of intrinsic human rights. Granted to us from the very spark of our existence. It is those rights, the freedom of thought, of organisation, of speech, of occupation, and so many more, those fundamental and inalienable rights upon which serves as the law of nature. They are the basis of the Crescent Moon's struggle, and dare they be the basis of the whole struggle of the whole China Democratic League.\n\nThe Chinese Constitution must be the first in the world that backs up its democratic embellishments with true citizen's democracy. For a free and truly democratic system must place human rights before even the paper they are demarcated upon. If a man so much so has a thought in his mind, there is but the desire to express such a thought. And if there is such one desire, it cannot simply be denied. Sic semper tyrannis; humankind must be allowed to exert itself free and willing, not be cowed into that of what other's desire.

Patrolling the Mountains
With the ousting of the rotten structure of Tang Jiyao's regime from the province, it has become evidently clear to the chiefs of the National Revolutionary Army that there remains holdouts within Yunnan's mountainous terrain. Pockmarked by deep valleys and assortments of titanic stone behemoths, Yunnan is the epitome of the Chinese interior's rugged terrain. We shall deploy NRA soldiers to eject any remaining guerillas from the province.

Once the leading force of Republicanism in the South, the Yunnan Clique finds itself humbled by the injustices of time. Forced to kneel at the foot of the Beijing Government, Governor Tang Jiyao finds his government deadlocked in a struggle against the remnants of the Kuomintang forces in Guizhou. Styling himself the leader of the Federalist Movement, Tang seeks to not only crush the KMT rebels, but carry out unification on his terms. Will the heir of National Protection see the Federalist banner fly across the Middle Kingdom, or shall the dream of the National Revolution be reborn with the flame of vengeance?

The Stacked House of Cards
§MThe Yunnan Clique§!\nSurrounding the delicate balance struck within §YYunnan§! are the various disparate political factions of the province. With the core and incumbency held by §aTang Jiyao's§! eponymous §aTang Clique§!, they pose to be the current face of provincial politics. Loyal directly to §PCai E's§! successor, §aTang Jiyao§!, the §aTang Clique's§! past is as marred as its leader's. Espousing both authoritarian and progressive policies with the ultimate goal of promoting §YFederalism§!, the §aTang Clique§! endeavours to secure the support of reformist intellectuals whilst still maintaining the loyalty of the gentry and officers. Similarly related is the §cPeople's Government Party (Minzhidang)§!, the successor to §aTang's§! earlier §cDemocratic Party (Minzhudang)§!, representing the Governor's more reformist, democratic and conservative approach inspired by §cLiang Qichao§!, §cZhang Shizhao§!, and §cZhang Taiyan§!.\n\nRunning in tandem in the pursuit of democracy is the noble §lCrescent Moon Society§!, formed as a collection of Anglo-American educated intellectuals who wrote for §lCrescent Moon Magazine§!. Often coming into conflict with left wing writers due to their adoption of a more moderate and modern conservative outlook of Chinese Culture, the §lCrescent Moon Acolytes§! soon began to promote a humanistic form of constitutionalism, with a focus on human rights and education.\n\nIn conjunction there remains the §PHu Ruoyu§! and §gLong Yun§! Cliques, centred around their eponymous figures. Adopting various forms of semi-progressive governmental outlooks, the warlordist cliques truly desire only to rule at the top, strengthen Yunnan, and persist within the province, at least on the surface. Counted among them are various minor interest groups, such as the §mYunnan Chamber of Commerce§!, the §nYoung China Party§!, and others.\n\n§MThe Kuomintang§!\nWithin the §kKuomintang's§! remnant regime that has consolidated itself in §YGuizhou§! remain many factions of disparate ideological interpretations of the Three Principles of the People, and the §aGuofu§!'s will. Beside loyalists of the Old Right, the Guizhou §kKMT§! feature the heartbed of the New Right sect of the party, under its chief ideological theorist §aDai Jitao§!. However the true reigns of power rest with the descendants of §PChiang Kai-shek§!, in the form of the §PWhampoa Clique§! led by §PHe Yingqin§!. Through the promotion of §aDai's§! palingenetic ultranationalism claimed to be sourced from traditional Chinese beliefs, §PHe Yingqin§! seeks to revitalise China in pursuit of the National Revolution.\n\nDue to §aDai's§! efforts, the Zhejiang Society of Revolutionary Comrades, currently headed by the §aChen brothers§!, has aspirations to coalesce into the informal entity of the §aCentral Club Clique§!, technocratics with their own \

Returning to the Spiritual Root
The Northwest frontier of China is but an untapped cornucopia of resources and virtue. It must merely be tapped by the Central Government. Securing both China's borders, and instilling a sense of pride within the spiritual hotspots of the nation, the Kuomintang have begun a programme of careful cultivation within the Northwest territories, ensuring to modernise whilst maintaining the delicate balance within the region.
